pmg_base_building_food_industry_grain_current = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_active_production_method = pm_bakery
        }
        value = pm_bakery_grain
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_active_production_method = pm_sweeteners
        }
        value = pm_sweeteners_grain
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_active_production_method = pm_baking_powder
        }
        value = pm_baking_powder_grain
    }
    else = {
        value = 0.0
    }
    multiply = building_work_efficiency
}

state_grain_production_if_no_pmg_base_building_food_industry = {
	value = state.sg:grain.state_goods_production
    if = {
        limit = {
            pmg_base_building_food_industry_grain_current > 0.0
        }
	subtract = pmg_base_building_food_industry_grain_current
    }
}

state_grain_consumption_if_no_pmg_base_building_food_industry = {
	value = state.sg:grain.state_goods_consumption
    if = {
        limit = {
            pmg_base_building_food_industry_grain_current < 0.0
        }
	add = pmg_base_building_food_industry_grain_current
    }
}

market_grain_production_if_no_pmg_base_building_food_industry = {
	value = market.mg:grain.market_goods_sell_orders
    if = {
        limit = {
            pmg_base_building_food_industry_grain_current > 0.0
        }
	subtract = pmg_base_building_food_industry_grain_current
        multiply = state.market_access
    }
}

market_grain_consumption_if_no_pmg_base_building_food_industry = {
	value = market.mg:grain.market_goods_buy_orders

    }

    }
    else_if = {

        }
        value = pm_patent_stills_glass
    }
    else = {
        value = 0.0
    }
    multiply = building_work_efficiency
}

pmg_base_building_airport_radios_current = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_active_production_method = pm_private_charters
        }
        value = pm_private_charters_radios
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_active_production_method = pm_regional_routes
        }
        value = pm_regional_routes_radios
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_active_production_method = pm_domestic_routes
        }
        value = pm_domestic_routes_radios
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_active_production_method = pm_international_routes
        }
        value = pm_international_routes_radios
    }
    else = {
        value = 0.0
    }
    multiply = building_work_efficiency
}

state_radios_production_if_no_pmg_base_building_airport = {
	value = state.sg:radios.state_goods_production
    if = {
        limit = {
            pmg_base_building_airport_radios_current > 0.0
        }
	subtract = pmg_base_building_airport_radios_current
    }
}

state_radios_consumption_if_no_pmg_base_building_airport = {
	value = state.sg:radios.state_goods_consumption
    if = {
        limit = {
            pmg_base_building_airport_radios_current < 0.0
        }
	add = pmg_base_building_airport_radios_current
    }
}

market_radios_production_if_no_pmg_base_building_airport = {
	value = market.mg:radios.market_goods_sell_orders
    if = {
        limit = {
            pmg_base_building_airport_radios_current > 0.0
        }
	subtract = pmg_base_building_airport_radios_current
        multiply = state.market_access
    }
}

market_radios_consumption_if_no_pmg_base_building_airport = {
	value = market.mg:radios.market_goods_buy_orders
    if = {
        limit = {
            pmg_base_building_airport_radios_current < 0.0
        }
	add = pmg_base_building_airport_radios_current
        multiply = state.market_access
    }
}
